## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

### No. 4: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

### No. 5: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt designed to generate an image of a vintage United States patent document from the late 1800s. It specifies details like precise technical drawings, handwritten annotations, aged paper texture, foxing stains, an embossed seal, and a wax stamp, making it ideal for historical or archival aesthetics.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A vintage patent document for {argument name="invention" default="INVENTION"}, styled after late 1800s United States Patent Office filings. The page features precise technical drawings with numbered callouts (Fig. 1, Fig. 2, Fig. 3) showing front, side, and exploded views. Handwritten annotations in fountain-pen ink describe mechanisms. The paper is aged ivory with foxing stains and soft fold creases. An official embossed seal and red wax stamp appear in the corner. A hand-signed inventor's name and date appear at the bottom. The entire image feels like a recovered archival documentâ€”authoritative, historic, and slightly mysterious.
```

### No. 7: AI Agent Development 'Swamp' Diagram Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON-based prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 'Swamp' diagram (a popular internet meme format) illustrating the circular nature of getting stuck in AI Agent development. The prompt defines the diagram's structure, style (simple, cute editorial), layout (straight intro track leading into a clockwise loop), and specific nodes with characters, visuals, and dialogue/thought terms.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
diagram:
  title: "{argument name="diagram title" default="The Cycle of the Generative AI Agent Development Swamp"}"
  style:
    character: "simple_editorial_cute"
    tone: "light_like_original"
    line: "soft_round"
    shading: "flat_minimal"
    palette: "muted_editorial"
    background: "light_beige_or_white"

  rule:
    first_character_only: "Only the first person is different"
    others_same_character: "All others are the same person"
    anxiety_requires_tech_terms: true
    dialogue_tone: "Maintain the short, light phrasing of the original diagram"

layout:
  intro_track: "The upper section is a straight line (left to right), then drops down to join the loop"
  loop_track: "Arranged as a loop (ring), with arrows curving clockwise along the circumference"

nodes:
  # ===== Upper Section: Straight Introduction =====
  - id: A
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_left"
    actor: "Different person (Senior Engineer)"
    visual: "Pointing at a laptop"
    item: "AI Agent Demo Screen"
    says: "It'll make you happy."
    arrow_to: { id: B, shape: "straight", direction: "right" }

  - id: B
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_center"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Waving lightly"
    says: "Even a simple agent..."
    arrow_to: { id: C, shape: "straight", direction: "right" }

  - id: C
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_right"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Executing sample code"
    item: "LangChain / CrewAI Sample"
    arrow_to: { id: D, shape: "straight", direction: "down" }

  # ===== D: Awakening Point =====
  - id: D
    zone: "connector"
    position: "right_outer_before_loop"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual:
      face: "Eyes wide open (cute)"
      effect: "Small flash of inspiration line"
      posture: "Leaning forward"
    state: "Awakening"
    says: "Agents, this is insane..."
    micro_text: "(Wakes up here)"
    arrow_to:
      id: E
      shape: "gentle_curve"
      direction: "down_into_ring"

  # ===== Loop Start (Must rotate from here) =====
  - id: E
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_right_upper"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Holding head in hands (cute)"
    state: "Anxiety/Irritation Begins"
    says: "Irritated"
    thought_terms:
      - "Prompt Design"
      - "Tool Selection"
      - "Memory Design"
    thought_text: "It's not working as intended..."
    arrow_to: { id: F, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: F
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_right_lower"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Surrounded by code and logs"
    state: "Irritation Settles In"
    says: "In a state of irritation"
    callout: "Loop! Runaway! Hallucination!"
    thought_terms:
      - "RAG"
      - "Function Calling"
      - "Tool-Use"
    arrow_to: { id: G, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: G
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_bottom"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Covered in sticky notes and diagrams"
    says: "The body gradually develops tolerance, and usage increases."
    items:
      - "Agent Architecture Diagram"
      - "Role Assignment Memo"
      - "State Transition Flow"
    arrow_to: { id: H, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: H
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_left_lower"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Works well, small fist pump"
    state: "Temporary Satisfaction"
    says: "Desire is temporarily satisfied"
    arrow_to: { id: I, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: I
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_left_upper"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Thinking again"
    state: "Obsession/Thought Occupation"
    says: "Thinking about the agent
```

### No. 9: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 10: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

### No. 3: Profile / Avatar - Hyper-realistic mirror selfie prompt with detailed material physics and identity locking

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed image generation prompt designed to create an extremely realistic, raw, high-contrast mirror selfie. It specifies strict identity locking, bio-fidelity for skin textures (TrueLens physics), precise outfit material realism (vacuum-tight jersey knit), and environmental details like realistic mirror imperfections and a sharp background, aiming for an unedited social media dump aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
(Vertical 9:16 smartphone aspect ratio). A raw, high-contrast mirror selfie captured with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. Everything is SHARP and in focus from the ornate mirror frame to the wooden textures in the background.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics: visible micro-pores, a natural "satin-finish" glow, and fine peach fuzz catching the light ONLY along the jawline.
Expression: Looking into the mirror with a confident, calm gaze and neutral, full lips.
Silhouette Calibration: Prioritize a dominant structural bust volume and an aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist. Maintain a symmetrical and fit anatomical depth.
Outfit & Material Realism:

Clothing: A skin-tight, jet-black jersey-knit long-sleeved dress. The neckline is styled asymmetrical, sliding off her RIGHT shoulder to reveal her collarbone.
Tension: The fabric shows extreme elastic tension and a vacuum-tight fit, creating realistic micro-folds and "tension lines" that highlight her fit silhouette and the physical interaction between the textile and her form.
Accessories: A delicate silver chain necklace with interlocking double-circle pendants resting on her dÃ©colletage.
Pose & Composition:

Pose: A classic indoor mirror selfie. She is standing with a slight hip-pop to emphasize the S-curve of her physique.
Action: Her LEFT HAND holds an iPhone 17 Pro (with a prominent circular grip/PopSocket on the back) at chest level, capturing the reflection.
Environment & Social Realism:

Mirror: Captured through an ornate octagonal gold-gilt framed mirror. Crucially, the glass features realistic imperfections: faint water spots, dust particles, and minor smudges that catch the light for a "raw evidence" look.
Background (SHARP): A domestic bathroom setting. Behind her, a dark wood-grain door and a neutral-toned wall are perfectly IN FOCUS. The chrome handle of a sink faucet is visible at the bottom of the frame.
Quality: Raw unedited social-media dump aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible digital grain in the deep shadows, 8k resolution.
```

### No. 4: Profile / Avatar - Chibi Character 'Tehepero' Pose Generation Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a chibi character performing the 'Tehepero' pose (winking and sticking out the tongue slightly). subject:

```
      - "chibi character"

      - "winking the right eye"
      - "tongue slightly sticking out upwards from the corner of the mouth ('Tehepero')"

      - "lightly tapping the high side of the head with the right fist"
      - "left arm is stretched straight downwards"

  body_orientation:
    torso:
      - "The front of the body is not completely facing the camera, but slightly angled (3/4 view)"

    direction: "looking at the camera"
    quality:
      - "soft frontal gaze"
      - "gazing at the viewer"
      - "gentle eye contact"

  camera_and_composition:
    angle:
      - "high angle"
      - "looking down from above, but the face is clearly visible"
    perspective:
      - "exaggerated perspective"
      - "strong foreshortening (foreground appears large, background appears small)"
    lens:
      focal_length_equivalent: "24mm equivalent"
      distance: "camera is close to the subject"

      - "full body included"

      - "simple white background"
```

### No. 6: Profile / Avatar - Raw Wide-Angle Glitter Dress Selfie

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical prompt for generating a raw, high-contrast, wide-angle smartphone selfie aesthetic, emphasizing hyper-realistic skin physics, aggressive body contouring, and harsh flash lighting, with a critical constraint of zero artificial bokeh and sharp focus throughout the entire frame.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
(Vertical 9:16 smartphone aspect ratio). A raw, high-contrast handheld 0.5x wide-angle selfie captured with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. Everything is SHARP and in focus from her glossy lips to the fabric of the sofa.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity skin physics: visible micro-pores, natural "satin-finish" night hydration, and ultra-glossy, plump lips. Fine peach fuzz is visible along the jawline.
Expression: A confident, heavy-lidded seductive gaze with a soft smirk directed at the lens.
Silhouette Calibration: Prioritize a dominant structural bust volume and substantial, thick-toned leg presence. Focus on the aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist.
Outfit & Physicality:

Clothing: A skin-tight, {argument name="dress color" default="Champagne-Gold"} Glittery Strapless Mini Dress.
Tension: The shimmery, reflective fabric shows extreme elastic tension and vacuum-tight fit, creating realistic micro-folds at the waist and highlighting her fit, symmetrical proportions.
Accessories: A delicate gold chain necklace with a small blue and white "Evil Eye" (Nazar) pendant resting on her collarbone.
Physics: Realistic skin-to-surface compression (thigh squish) is visible where her legs meet the sofa.
Pose & Composition:

Pose: She is reclining back into a sofa. High-angle downward POV (0.5x) looking at her torso and legs. Her body is slightly twisted to maximize the S-curve silhouette.
Action: Her RIGHT ARM is visible in the frame, holding the phone high for the selfie.
Environment & Lighting:

Lighting: Direct, harsh indoor lighting (mimicking a smartphone flash). The light creates brilliant starburst reflections on the glittery dress and a high-key glow on her skin.
Background (SHARP): A detailed domestic setting. A grey textured fabric cushion and the beige leather-grain of the sofa back are all perfectly IN FOCUS. No artificial blur.
Quality: Raw unedited "fit-check" social-media dump aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible digital grain in the deep shadows, 8k resolution.
```

### No. 9: Profile / Avatar - Raw High-Definition Printed Portrait Aesthetic Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed prompt designed to emulate a raw, high-definition photograph of a physical printed portrait, capturing the texture of the paper and ink. It focuses heavily on realism, specific lighting (harsh studio flash), and includes a creative text overlay, ideal for generating yearbook or vintage magazine archive aesthetics.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
(3:4). A raw, high-definition photograph of a physical printed portrait taken with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. Everything is SHARP and in focus, capturing the physical textural reality of the paper grain and the ink-on-page in high resolution.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics as captured through high-end printed ink: visible micro-pores, natural "satin-finish" glow muted by paper texture, and fine peach fuzz along the jawline.
Expression: A perfectly aligned, symmetrical head-and-shoulders yearbook-style pose. Neutral but confident expression with a magnetic, "main character" gaze looking directly into the lens.
Silhouette Calibration: Despite the formal school tailoring, amplify the dominant structural bust volume and the aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist. Ensure the fit of the uniform highlights a high-impact, fit physique.
Outfit & Material Realism:

Clothing: A dark navy blue structured blazer with white piping, a crisp white collared shirt, and a dark navy striped silk tie.
Tension: The blazer and shirt show extreme material tension and a vacuum-tight fit, creating realistic physical interaction and "tension lines" that highlight her fit, symmetrical upper silhouette and anatomical depth.
The Printed Aesthetic (Hardware Emulation):

Surface Texture: The image features an authentic semi-gloss paper sheen with thin, realistic diagonal lamination glares reflecting off the ink surface across the cheeks and chest.
Ink Physics: Visible ink-absorption softening at the edges (not digital blur), fine paper grain texture, and a gentle warm undertone typical of vintage magazine archives. It looks like a scanned physical object.
Lighting & Composition:

Lighting: Direct frontal harsh studio flash (ID style). Even exposure with bright, sharp eye catchlights and minimal shadows, creating a flat but clean professional portrait look.
Background (SHARP): A flat, textured cool-blue studio backdrop, showing realistic ink-on-paper depth.
Creative "Pinterest" Text Overlay:

Center-aligned below the portrait in an ink-printed bold serif font: "{argument name="main text" default="MOST LIKELY TO..."}"
Below in smaller, elegant italic subtext: "{argument name="subtext" default="â€œBe the reason you check your phone every 5 minutes.â€"}"
The text features slightly imperfect ink bleeding and natural letter-spacing, mimicking an authentic high-end physical printing process.
Quality: Raw scan/photo-of-print aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible paper fiber and digital ISO noise in the shadows, 8k resolution, looks physically touchable.
```

### No. 32: Infographic / Edu Visual - Visual Infographic of Ancient Chinese Official Ranks and Attire

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This is a detailed, historical infographic prompt designed to visualize and break down the ranking system of official attire in ancient China, specifically focusing on the Qing Dynasty. It requests a 16:9 horizontal composition in the style of ancient historical diagrams and illustrated books, comparing the uniforms of nine officials from the first to the ninth rank. The prompt specifies detailed elements like the embroidered rank badges (Buzi), court beads (Chaozhu), hat ornaments (Dingdai Hualing), and dragon robes (Mangpao), along with explanatory tables and historical context, making it suitable for educational content on Chinese history and culture.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Create a historical diagram-style infographic, 16:9 horizontal composition, titled "Visual Deconstruction of the Ancient Chinese Official Attire Ranking System." Adopt the aesthetic of ancient canonical diagrams and draw in the style of illustrations from ancient books. The image should display a comparison of the official uniforms of nine ranks of officials from the {argument name="dynasty" default="Qing Dynasty"}, arranged from left to right by rank: nine standing figures from the first to the ninth rank. Above each figure, use fine-line painting (Gongbi) to label the "Buzi (Rank Badge) Pattern" (First Rank Crane, Second Rank Golden Pheasant, Third Rank Peacock... Ninth Rank Quail; civil officials use flying birds, military officials use fierce beasts), with a close-up magnifying glass effect highlighting the embroidery details of the Buzi. Below the figures, label the "Chaozhu (Court Bead) Material" (First Rank Eastern Pearl, Second Rank Coral, Third Rank Sapphire... decreasing by rank), "Dingdai Hualing (Hat Ornament)" (Ruby/Coral/Sapphire/Crystal, etc., distinguished by color blocks), and "Mangpao (Dragon Robe) Pattern" (Nine Dragons/Five Claws/Four Claws, using diagrams to illustrate the difference in claw count). The top of the image features a "Rank Identification Quick Reference Chart": a table comparing the differences across 5 dimensions (Buzi, Dingdai, Chaozhu, Mangpao, Waist Belt) for all 9 ranks, with each cell marked by a small icon and text. The bottom of the image features "Historical Trivia": labeling "Why civil officials used flying birds and military officials used fierce beasts" (civil service requires soaring high, military service requires bravery), "The political meaning of the Hualing" (being granted a Hualing signifies imperial favor), and "Color Restrictions" (commoners were forbidden from wearing yellow or bright yellow). The very bottom includes a timeline showing the "Evolution of Official Attire through Dynasties": thumbnail sketches illustrating the style changes from the Han, Tang, Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties. All text must be in Chinese: the top title uses the Small Seal Script font "Official Attire Rank Diagram: The Power Code Worn on the Body," and the bottom caption states "The clothing system is the visual representation of the feudal hierarchy." Use traditional official attire colors for the palette. The overall presentation should focus on historical institutions and clothing culture, suitable for historical education and cultural research.
```

Left section: historical precedents and influences, showing ancestor instruments with lineage lines connecting them, maker's marks, and period photographs. Center section: the subject instrument in exploded view, every component separated and floating, wood species identified, varnish layers shown in cross-section, acoustic properties annotated with frequency response curves and tap tone locations. Title block reading â€œ{argument name="instrument name" default="[INSTRUMENT NAME]"} â€” {argument name="maker name" default="[MAKER]"}, [CITY], [YEAR], OPUS [NUMBER]".

### No. 35: Infographic / Edu Visual - Scientific Theory Visualization Generator

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-phase prompt designed to visualize abstract scientific theories or formulas (like black holes) as photorealistic, impossible architectural structures. It starts with a 2D notation medium (e.g., chalk on a blackboard) and extrudes the lines into a solid 3D structure, featuring a tiny scientist observing the creation.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instructions> do this for {argument name="scientific concept" default="black holes"}
  Input Variable:   {argument name="theorem or formula" default="[Theorem / Formula]"}
Phase 1: Schematic Decomposition
Analyze the Notation: Identify the primary visual language of the scientist (Chalk on blackboard? Ink on parchment? Pencil on graph paper?).
Identify the "Structure": If this theory were a building, what would it look like?
Logic: Chaos Theory -> Fractal Spire. Thermodynamics -> Engine Block.
Phase 2: The Dimensional Transition
The Base: A flat surface covered in the [Notation Medium] (e.g., a slate blackboard covered in chalk equations).
The Extrusion: The chalk lines physically lift off the surface. They begin as white wireframes, then gain opacity, then gain texture.
The Climax: At the top of the image, the wireframes have fully solidified into a photorealistic, impossible structure representing the theory.
The Observer: A tiny, scale-model figure of the scientist stands on the flat "2D" section, looking up in awe at the massive "3D" structure they have summoned.
Output: High-Angle Isometric, "Architectural Visualization" style, stark contrast between sketchy lines and solid mass.
</instructions>
```

### No. 37: Infographic / Edu Visual - Seed to Shelf Diorama Flowchart Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-step instruction prompt for visualizing the lifecycle of a product (like coffee or a diamond ring) using a miniature photography aesthetic. It requires generating a single image featuring a 'Seed to Shelf' flowchart diorama on a vintage map, with three distinct 3D vignettes (Origin, Process, Destination) connected by a winding conveyor belt filled with the product, all rendered at HO Scale (1:87) with tilt-shift effect.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instruction>
  1. Analyze Input Variable:  
Input A is a Global Commodity with a distinct production lifecycle (e.g., Coffee, Chocolate/Cocoa, Wine, Denim/Cotton).
Deconstruct the lifecycle into   3 Distinct Stages  :
   Stage 1 (The Origin):  The agricultural source (e.g., Coffee Plantation, Cacao Trees).
   Stage 2 (The Process):  The industrial transformation (e.g., Roasting Plant, Fermentation Vats).
   Stage 3 (The Destination):  The retail experience (e.g., A Hipster Cafe, A Chocolatier Shop).
2.  Container (The Map Table):
Goal: A "Seed to Shelf" Flowchart Diorama.
The Base: A large, vintage World Map (blue oceans, pastel continents) laid flat on a wooden dining table.
The Spine: A raised, winding S-Shaped Chute/Conveyor snakes through the center of the image, physically connecting the three stages.
The Flow: The chute is filled with the product, which visually transforms as it moves down the path (e.g., Red Coffee Cherries at the top 
â†’
â†’
 Brown Roasted Beans in the middle 
â†’
â†’
 Fine Ground Powder at the bottom).
3. The Vignettes (The Stations):
Construct a 3D diorama "Island" at each key point of the S-curve:
Top Station (Origin): A square patch of terrain sitting on the map (e.g., South America). Detailed crops, trees, and farmers harvesting the raw material.
Middle Station (Process): A compact industrial facility sitting on the map (e.g., Europe/USA). Metallic roasters, silos, smoke stacks, and factory workers.
Bottom Station (Destination): An architectural Cutaway Box. The front wall is removed to reveal the interior of a shop (e.g., Espresso machines, tiny customers sitting at tables, baristas serving).
4. The Narrative Scale (The Workers):
Scale: 1:87 (HO Scale) miniature figures.
Action: The figures are not just standing; they are actively moving the product from the "Station" into the "Chute" (e.g., Farmers dumping baskets of cherries into the stream, Factory workers shoveling beans).
5. Lighting & Atmosphere:
Camera Angle: High-Angle Perspective (45-60 degrees). Looking down the length of the table.
Lighting: Natural Daylight. Bright, cheerful, and even. Shadows fall softly on the map.
Depth of Field: Tilt-Shift effect. The top and bottom edges of the table are slightly blurred to make the models look tiny.
Output: ONE image, Vertical Aspect Ratio (4:5), Miniature Photography, Educational Diorama aesthetic.
</instruction>
```

### No. 41: Infographic / Edu Visual - Kinetic Sculpture of Scientific Discovery in a Lab Notebook

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly creative and detailed prompt for generating a single image that visualizes a scientific discovery as a kinetic sculpture rising from an aged lab notebook. It requires blending steampunk-inspired brass and glass apparatus with handwritten notes and sketches, including a tiny figurine of the scientist and a subtle glowing element to symbolize the 'eureka' moment, rendered in an industrial scientific photography style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Role:
Science Historian & Kinetic Sculpture Engineer

Input:
Scientific Discovery: {argument name="scientific discovery" default="{{DISCOVERY}}"}
Primary Scientist: {argument name="scientist name" default="{{SCIENTIST_NAME}}"}

Year: {{YEAR}}
Lab Location: {{LOCATION}}

Phase 1: Concept Analysis

Identify the defining eureka moment behind {{DISCOVERY}}
Briefly imply earlier failed attempts through visual cues

Select the key physical apparatus used or symbolized in this discovery (e.g. telescope, prism, microscope, equation, clock, lens)

Phase 2: Visual Execution

Goal:
A single 1x1 frame showing a working â€œlab notebook contraptionâ€ frozen mid-discovery.

Scene Rules:

Base:
An open, aged lab notebook on a wooden desk. Coffee stains, handwritten equations, rough sketches, and marginal notes fill the pages.

The Machine:
A functional brass and glass apparatus rises directly from the notebook pages. Steampunk-inspired but scientifically grounded.

The Process:
The apparatus actively demonstrates {{DISCOVERY}}

Examples: light bending, gears rotating, particles flowing, rings orbiting, waves oscillating.

The Scientist:
A tiny, realistic figurine of {{SCIENTIST_NAME}} in period-accurate lab clothing, holding a fountain pen and taking notes.

The Failure:
Crossed-out equations, torn sketches, and crumpled paper scattered near the notebook.

The Eureka:
One subtle glowing element (LED, filament, beam of light, energized ring) symbolizing the breakthrough moment.

The Label:
Handwritten in fountain pen style on the notebook page:
â€œ{{SCIENTIST_NAME}} | {{DISCOVERY}} | {{YEAR}} | {{LOCATION}}â€

Era Props:
Period-accurate tools such as a slide rule, telegram, brass compass, glass tubes, Bunsen burner, vacuum tubes, or notebooks.

Style & Output

Composition: Single frame, centered subject, square 1x1

Lighting: Dramatic side lighting, warm highlights, deep shadows

Texture: Brass, glass, paper fibers, ink stains clearly visible

Photography Style: Industrial scientific photography, cinematic realism

Mood: Quiet intensity, intellectual tension, frozen moment of discovery
Quality: Ultra-detailed, macro realism, shallow depth of field
```

### No. 42: Infographic / Edu Visual - Deconstructed Culinary Promotional Poster

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured prompt designed for generating a premium culinary promotional poster featuring a deconstructed meal, such as Tiramisu. It specifies a pure black background, layered arrangement following the cooking sequence, detailed texture descriptions for each ingredient layer, and elegant annotations.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{argument name="dish name" default="Tiramisu"}], [vertical] arrangement, premium culinary promotional poster with pure black background (#000000), presenting a deconstructed layered display of this dish. Arranged from top to bottom or left to right following the cooking sequence. 
    
    Visual Structure: 5-7 layers, showcasing the complete deconstruction from raw ingredients to finished dish. One end features sauce or seasoning liquid, middle layers include aromatics, main ingredients, and key seasonings, with the finished dish at the other end. 
    
    Each layer separated by appropriate spacing to highlight textures and details; the finished dish layer maintains significantly larger gap from adjacent layers to create dramatic final presentation. 
    
    Ingredient Textures: 
    
    - Sauce layer: Showcase clean, premium sauces or seasonings - Aromatics layer: Vibrant colors, floating weightlessly, emanating warm fragrance, tangibly realistic texture - Main ingredient layer: Clear textures, distinct layers, showcasing natural grain of premium ingredients, fresh and dewy
    
     - Seasoning layer: Crystal clear, well-defined granules, 
    
    warm luster - Finished dish layer: Glossy and appetizing, tender texture, coated in rich sauce, surface slightly trembling, steam rising, aroma seemingly penetrating the frame. 
    
    The finished dish should be slightly larger than other decomposed layers Visual Style: - All elements floating against pure black background, no white base or platform 
    
    - Uniform 45-degree angle photography, highly realistic style - Finished dish placed in appropriate vessel, consistent angle with decomposed layers above Annotations: Elegant labels with refined arrows pointing to each component, labeling each layer's ingredients or seasonings. 
    
    Atmosphere Details: 
    
    - Transition zones feature subtle floating wisps of steam, oil droplets, and spice particles gently descending, enhancing dynamism and authentic cooking atmosphere 
    
    - Soft highlights near finished dish, echoing the glossy sheen of ingredients and glaze-like quality of the sauce
```

```
<instructions> 
Role:   Science Historian & Kinetic Sculpture Engineer

  Input:   [{argument name="scientific discovery" default="Scientific Discovery, e.g., DNA Structure, Theory of Relativity"}]

  Phase 1: Analysis  
1. Identify the "eureka moment" and the failed attempts before it
2. Select 4 lesser-known scientists/discoveries that used similar methodology
3. Extract the physical apparatus used in the discovery (microscope, prism, blackboard equation)

  Phase 2: Execution  
  Goal:   2x2 Grid of "Working Lab Notebook Contraptions"

  Rules per Panel:  
-   The Base:   An open, coffee-stained lab notebook with handwritten equations/sketches
-   The Machine:   A functional brass and glass apparatus rises FROM the notebook pages (steampunk aesthetic)
-   The Process:   The machine actively demonstrates the discovery (gears turning, liquid flowing, light refracting)
-   The Scientist:   Tiny figurine in period lab coat taking notes with a fountain pen
-   The Failure:   Crossed-out attempts and crumpled paper nearby
-   The Eureka:   A single glowing element (LED) representing the breakthrough moment
-   The Label:   Fountain pen handwriting: "Scientist Name | Discovery | Year | Lab Location"
-   The Props:   Era-accurate items (telegram, slide rule, Bunsen burner, petri dishes)

  Output:   2x2 Grid, Industrial Scientific Photography, dramatic side lighting
</instructions>
```

### No. 56: YouTube Thumbnail - Nano Banana Pro Composition Techniques Prompts (3 Examples)

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A tutorial-style tweet explaining three advanced composition techniques for Nano Banana Pro: 1) using 'Text Anchors' to force negative space for thumbnails/posters, 2) using 'Physical Camera Work Specification' (like wide-angle, low-angle) for dynamic scenes, and 3) using 'Infographic Grid' for organized layouts like process diagrams. It includes executable prompts for each technique.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Role]
You are a professional graphic designer. Create a YouTube thumbnail.

[Composition Instructions]
- Split-screen composition, dividing the screen into left and right halves.
- Left side: A Japanese woman with a surprised expression (photorealistic style). Background is a dark office.
- Right side: A vibrant yellow background. Place the text â€œ{argument name="text" default="AI Revolution"}â€ in bold Gothic font in the center.
- Ensure sufficient negative space around the text to maximize visibility.

[Style]
A scene from an animated movie, cyberpunk

[Camera and Composition Settings]
- Lens: Use a wide-angle lens (24mm equivalent) to emphasize perspective.
- Angle: Extreme low angle (worm's-eye view). The character is viewed looking up from just above the ground.
- Placement: Place the character's left hand directly in front of the camera to exaggerate the sense of distance.
- Background: High-rise buildings sharply converge toward a vanishing point.

[Role]
You are a manual creator. Create {argument name="subject" default="how to make Okonomiyaki"}.

[Format]
Flat design infographic, 16:9

[Layout Instructions]
- A â€œ3-stepâ€ process diagram flowing from left to right.
- Step 1 (Left): Magnifying glass icon (Investigation).
- Step 2 (Center): Gear icon (Processing).
- Step 3 (Right): Light bulb icon (Solution).
- Connect each element with arrows and align them at equal intervals.
- Background is white, icons are unified in blue and orange key colors.
```

### No. 59: YouTube Thumbnail - Nano Banana Pro Image Generation Prompt for MBTI Character Visualization

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extensive image generation prompt for Nano Banana Pro, designed to visualize an MBTI personality type as an anime-style character. It takes the MBTI diagnosis results (type and reason) from a previous LLM analysis and uses them to customize a base character profile (anime girl with brown hair and red eyes). The prompt includes detailed instructions for UI layout (9:16 vertical image, text placement), character layering rules based on the 16 MBTI types (e.g., ENTJ gets a military-style jacket and a crown), and specific color themes for each MBTI group.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
## 1. Input Variables (Rewrite this)
Generate an illustration based on the following information.

User Information:
target_account: "{argument name="Account Name" default="@schnapoon"}"
mbti_type: {argument name="MBTI Type" default="ENTJ (Commander)"}
reason: "{argument name="Diagnosis Reason" default="Posts structurally share how to utilize AI tools and actively engage with users. Efficient prompt creation and creative idea proposals stand out, showing a leadership-oriented thought pattern."}"

Character Setting (base_character_profile):
Appearance: Anime-style girl. Brown medium hair, red eyes, slightly pointed teeth (giza-ba).

## 2. Generation Instructions
A. Overall Image Composition (UI Layout)
Generate a vertical 9:16 image. The background color is clean off-white (#F5F5F7).
The screen is composed of the following elements from top to bottom:

1. Header Text:
   Place the text `target_account` + "'s diagnosis result is" at the top of the screen.
   Color: Dark gray (#333333), Font size: Medium, Alignment: Center.

2. Main Character Illustration:
   Important (Consistency): Maintain the "physical features (face, hair, body type)" and "basic clothing (innerwear, bottoms, etc.)" of the `base_character_profile` without alteration.
   Changes (Layering): Express the individuality of each type by "layering" the specified outerwear, mantle, and decorations from "B. MBTI Style Definitions" below over the basic clothing.
   Presentation: Draw specified effects and floating items around the character.
   Style: High-quality anime coloring.

3. MBTI Type Label:
   Place the `mbti_type` text largely directly below the illustration.
   Color: Theme color of each type definition.
   Font: Bold for high visibility.

4. Diagnosis Reason Text Box:
   Place a white, rounded-corner box (card-like design) at the bottom of the screen.
   Write the `reason` text in Japanese inside it.
   Text color: Gray (#555555), Left-aligned, readable size.

B. MBTI Style Definitions (16 Types Layering Rules)
Apply the style matching the input `mbti_type` and add the following items over the basic clothing:

[Analysts - Purple/Dark Blue/Deep Red]
   INTJ (Architect):
       Layering: Black long coat or a chic jacket with a standing collar.
       Items: Chess pieces, hologram of blueprints.
   INTP (Logician):
       Layering: Lab coat (slightly disheveled), or a loose hoodie.
       Items: Flasks, floating mathematical formulas, gadget parts.
   ENTJ (Commander):
       Layering: Military-style Napoleon jacket, or a heavy mantle with a red lining.
       Items: Baton, crown-like decoration.
   ENTP (Debater):
       Layering: Unconventional design blazer, or a magician-like cape.
       Items: Microphone, smirking expression, jack-in-the-box effect.

[Diplomats - Green/Gold/Pastel]
   INFJ (Advocate):
       Layering: Hooded robe, or a mystical shawl.
       Items: Lantern, staff, mystical light particles.
   INFP (Mediator):
       Layering: Oversized knit cardigan, or a forest-girl style poncho.
       Items: Flower crown, butterflies, books.
   ENFJ (Protagonist):
       Layering: Hero-like mantle, shining brooch or sash on the chest.
       Items: Holy sword (light-shaped), halo-like effect.
   ENFP (Campaigner):
       Layering: Colorful patchwork vest, or a flashy scarf.
       Items: Balloons, confetti, party goods.

[Sentinels - Blue/White/Teal]
   ISTJ (Logistician):
       Layering: Neat navy blazer, armband.
       Items: Clipboard, glasses, neatly arranged documents.
   ISFJ (Defender):
       Layering: Clean apron, or medical coat/nurse uniform-style outerwear.
       Items: First aid kit, warm drink (tea, etc.).
   ESTJ (Executive):
       Layering: Formal suit jacket,
```

### No. 64: Comic / Storyboard - Hyper-realistic crossover image of Zenitsu Agatsuma from Demon Slayer

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, hyper-realistic prompt for Nano Banana Pro that generates an image of Zenitsu Agatsuma from the anime 'Demon Slayer' stepping out of a giant physical manga book, blending the 8K photo-realistic world with the black-and-white manga panel style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
An astonishing hyper-realistic 8K photograph capturing the moment {argument name="character name" default="Zenitsu Agatsuma"} from "{argument name="manga name" default="Demon Slayer"}" steps out of a giant physical manga book.

Zenitsu in the real world:
Zenitsu's image is photorealistic, with messy gold and orange hair, wearing a realistically textured Demon Slayer Corps uniform and his iconic yellow haori with white triangle patterns. His expression is determined, his eyes sharp, full of resolve, tightly gripping his Nichirin blade in its sheath. Half of his body has stepped onto the wooden bedroom floor, while the other half remains within the manga pages.
The giant manga book and interaction:
A giant, thick Japanese edition of "Demon Slayer" manga book is spread open on a slightly worn wooden floor. Zenitsu breaks the boundary of the paper, and the pages are violently torn, curled, and burst where he steps out, with paper scraps and toner flying in the air.

Details within the manga page (picture-in-picture):
The pages display an extremely authentic black-and-white Japanese manga style.
Style: Rough black ink lines, rich screentone textures for shading, exaggerated speed lines.

Layout: Strict Japanese right-to-left reading order, a surreal four-panel manga (yonkoma) spread.
Content: Inside the broken panel, a trapped, manga-style Zenitsu can be seen. He is wearing the same clothes, shedding noodle tears in the panel, frantically knocking on the borders of the manga panel, accompanied by large Japanese onomatopoeia like "å‡ºã‚‰ã‚Œãªã„!" (Can't get out!), "ãˆãˆãˆ!?", and "ãƒ‰ãƒ³ãƒ‰ãƒ³ãƒ‰ãƒ³" (Knocking sound). The manga version of him is watching the real-world version of himself tear the frame in terror.

Environment and lighting:
The bedroom background is soft-focused, with domestic items like bed legs and bookshelves. Natural afternoon light streams in from the side window, illuminating the edges of the torn paper and the fabric texture of Zenitsu's clothes, emphasizing the strong contrast between reality and the two-dimensional world.
```

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
The attached pink-haired woman is "Nagisa no Yosei Gibasa-chan" (Gibasa-chan the Fairy of the Shore).
Please create a four-panel manga where this character introduces herself. The four panels should follow the KishÅtenketsu structure and include a punchline.
- Nagisa no Yosei Gibasa-chan is a fairy of the seaweed called akamoku.
- The attached image of seaweed in the sea is akamoku. Please include an image that conveys the image of akamoku.
- All dialogue must be written vertically in Japanese.
- Speech bubbles should progress from right to left.
- "Gibasa" is a dialectal name for "akamoku."
- The attached image of food topped with something is akamoku rice. Akamoku rice is a typical way to eat akamoku, so please include a panel where Gibasa-chan is eating akamoku rice.
```

```
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",

    ]
  },

    "scene": "giant open comic book on the floor of a detailed aesthetic room",

    "walls": "comic art blending into real textures",

    ]
```

### No. 81: Product Marketing - Luxury minimalist product photography based on a reference image

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating high-end, minimalist commercial product photography in the style of luxury brand ads, using an uploaded reference image of the core product as the base.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Using my uploaded reference image as the base, generate a minimalist, high-quality commercial still life photograph with the aesthetic of a luxury brand advertisement.

Preserve the general shape, proportions, and main color scheme of the core product in the reference so that it is instantly recognizable as the same product, but upgrade the overall texture and atmosphere of the image, making it look like an ad for a top-tier international fragrance, skincare item, or high-end electronic product.

Use a vertical 4:5 composition. The background should be a large area of clean, neutral negative space, such as soft off-white, cool gray, or light beige, creating a quiet, restrained, and expensive studio environment. Apart from the core product and a minimal number of necessary supports, do not add any extra decorations. No clutter, no elaborate scene setupâ€”only keep very simple geometric supports (such as a plain white cube, a cylinder, or a thin transparent panel). The supports must be simple and low-profile, existing only to hold and accentuate the product.

Strongly emphasize the material details of the product, and let the lighting fully serve those materials:
Show frosted glass with a fine, soft matte texture, ceramics with a matte or slightly glazed feel, and polished metal with clean, sharp specular highlights. Liquids should have clearly visible viscosity and volume. Avoid any cheap plastic feel, complex patterns, or gaudy stickers; the overall material quality must feel cool, restrained, and luxurious.

Use professional studio lighting: mainly soft, diffused light from softboxes, plus precise rim light outlining the productâ€™s shape. The contours should be crisp and layered, and the shadows should be soft and clean, with no noise or dirty shadow patches. You may use a near-macro viewpoint, moving in closer to the product to highlight materials and details, while preserving ample negative space around the frame so the product can "speak for itself" in the emptiness.

Keep the overall color scheme neutral and calm. The productâ€™s own color can be slightly more saturated, making it the single visual focal point in the scene. Do not use exaggerated gradient backgrounds, flashy colored lighting, or e-commerce promo aesthetics. No large-price text, labels, or cartoon graphics.

The final result must be a high-resolution commercial key visual that looks ready for a magazine back cover or a high-end brand announcement poster: minimalist, quiet, high-end, with the core product confidently centered, surrounded by clean negative space and precisely controlled lighting.
```

### No. 88: Product Marketing - Studio Portrait with Digital UI Overlay

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A unique hybrid composition prompt combining a highly realistic, volumetrically lit studio portrait with a flat, clean digital graphics overlay, simulating a mobile phone browser interface that segments the subject, ideal for e-commerce or conceptual art.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Subject Reference: A full-body portrait of [INSERT SUBJECT NAME].
Scene Description: A full-body, centered portrait of the subject [INSERT POSE DESCRIPTION]. The subject has [INSERT EXPRESSION], staring directly at the camera. The immediate background behind the subject is a [INSERT BACKGROUND TYPE, e.g., seamless, pure high-key white studio backdrop]. Crucially, the subject is lit with volumetric studio lighting that creates deep definitions, realistic shadows, and a strong 3D quality on her body and the folds of the outfit, distinguishing her sharply from the flat background without casting shadows on the floor.

CRITICAL DETAIL (UI Layer): The entire photographic image is digitally layered beneath a simulated mobile phone browser interface overlay. Four distinct, clean, white, rectangular browser window elements are stacked vertically and angled slightly, segmenting the subject. Each window bar contains the sharp text '{argument name="link text" default="[INSERT LINK OR TEXT HERE]"}'. The area outside the active white browser windows is a solid, uniform, dark charcoal gray/black matte UI frame, with absolutely no light bleed or color gradients.

Style: Hybrid Composition: A highly realistic, three-dimensional studio photograph with deep color depth, overlaid with flat, clean digital graphics. Lighting Quality: Specific volumetric studio lighting focused ONLY on the subject. Soft, directional light from slightly off-center to sculpt the body and the rich texture of the fabric, creating depth. The background must remain completely flat.

Color Palette: High contrast. {argument name="outfit color" default="[INSERT OUTFIT COLOR]"} outfit against {argument name="background color" default="[INSERT BACKGROUND COLOR]"} backdrop, framed by the dark matte gray UI.

Texture and Mood: Realistic skin and rich fabric texture contrasting with the smooth digital elements of the UI. Intentional inclusion of subtle digital noise/grain to mimic a screen capture. Full body, centered portrait. Ensure the head and feet are fully within the frame before segmentation. Angle: Straight eye-level view, perpendicular to the subject.

Framing Elements: Four overlapping, white browser windows/tabs. The pose is elegant and fluid. The bottom interface elements (e.g., 'Private', 'Done') must be clean and visible. Focal Length: Standard portrait lens (approx. 50mm equivalent) for realistic proportions.

Camera Type: Simulated high-quality smartphone screen capture of a professional photo. Depth of Field: Shallow enough to focus sharply on the subject, allowing the background to be soft. Post Processing: Clean digital segmentation. Contrast adjusted to enhance depth.

Avoid Keywords: Floor shadows, flat lighting, 2D look, inconsistent UI color, bleeding colors, HDR, oversharpened. Location: Simulated E-commerce studio ([INSERT BACKGROUND TYPE]).
```

### No. 90: Product Marketing - Realistic Interior to Transparent Miniature Diorama Prompt

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This is the second part of the two-step prompt sequence, using the previously generated realistic interior image as a reference. The goal is to transform that realistic room into a highly detailed, transparent miniature architectural model or diorama, similar to a museum exhibit. The prompt emphasizes preserving the exact layout and proportions while focusing on high-end industrial design aesthetics, transparent acrylic/glass casing, realistic miniature materials, and sophisticated internal/external lighting contrast.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Based on the uploaded "realistic interior space" reference image, generate a "transparent miniature house display model."

[Core Display Concept]
- Transform the original realistic interior space into a "miniature-scale transparent architectural model"
- Like an architectural cross-section model displayed in a museum
- The house is completely enclosed in a transparent acrylic / glass shell
- The interior structure and furniture are fully visible

[Structure and Layout (Must be Strictly Retained)]
- Strictly inherit the interior layout and proportions from the reference image
- Wall positions, furniture placement, and circulation paths must be identical
- The room is scaled down entirely to a miniature proportion (e.g., 1:10 / 1:12)
- This is proportional scaling, not redesign

[Transparent Casing Design]
- Exterior is high-transparency acrylic or glass material
- Rounded corners, clearly visible thickness
- Local use of cutaway / angled structures for easy viewing of the interior
- The transparent casing does not obstruct the main interior view

[Interior Representation (Miniature but Realistic)]
- All furniture is scaled down proportionally
- Materials remain realistic: wood grain, fabric, metal
- Retain a sense of real life, not a toy feel
- Lighting fixtures, plants, and ornaments are clearly visible

[Lighting System (Key Focus)]
- Warm-toned micro-lights inside (like model lights)
- Neutral or cool-toned display lights outside
- Creates a high-end display contrast of warm interior and cool exterior
- Gently glowing but not dazzling

[Display Environment]
- Placed on a minimalist pedestal / museum display stand
- Clean background (light gray / dark gray / black)
- Includes a real scale reference (like the stand's shadow)

[Visual Style]
- Hyper-realistic
- High-end industrial design aesthetic
- Looks like a display piece from Apple / Muji / an architectural firm
- Not toy-like, not cartoonish

[Photography and Composition]
- Professional product photography or architectural model photography
- Medium-close shot composition, slightly overhead view
- Shallow depth of field, blurred background
- Clear focus on the transparent miniature house itself

[Technical Requirements]
- Ultra-high definition details
- High refractive index, realistic glass representation
- Correct reflections and perspective
- No people, no text, no watermarks

Displayed as an art installation, possessing contemporary design and collectible value
Healing, exquisite, visually striking effect that immediately captures attention
Avoid toy texture, avoid plastic feel, emphasize architectural model and industrial design texture
High transparency, clear refractive edges, clean glass
Interior lighting clearly visible, like a miniature model lighting system
```

### No. 112: Game Asset - Cyber-Industrial Exoskeleton Object Transformation Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A system instruction prompt designed to reimagine any input object (like a sneaker or a skull) as a complex, high-performance Cyber-Industrial Assembly. It specifies deconstruction into segmented carbon fiber panels, internal mechanics with glowing industrial cabling, and detailed greebles, rendered as a photorealistic 3D product shot with specific studio lighting and Octane Bloom effects.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instructions> 
Input Variable: {argument name="object" default="[INSERT OBJECT]"} (e.g., A Sneaker, A Human Skull, A Cheeseburger, The Letter 'A')

System Instruction:
Reimagine the Input Object as a complex, high-performance Cyber-Industrial Assembly.

1.  Deconstruction:
   The Shell: Replace the object's natural skin with Matte Black Carbon Fiber and Gunmetal Grey Polymer.
   The Segmentation: The object is not solid. It is segmented into distinct panels (like Iron Man armor or a high-end camera body), held together by visible Hex Bolts and Rivets.
   The Gaps: Between the panels, leave small gaps to reveal the internal mechanics.

2.  Internal Mechanics :
   The Piping: Where organic veins or structure would be, insert Bundled Industrial Cabling and Braided Steel Hoses.
   The Flow: These cables must look functional, routing power from a central core to the extremities of the object.
   The Glow (The Soul):
       Color: Identify the "Spirit Color" of the object (e.g., Burger = Amber/Orange; Skull = Cyan/Blue; Sneaker = Neon Green).
       Source: Hidden LED strips and neon tubes run parallel to the cables, casting a strong internal glow that spills out from the panel gaps.

3. The Narrative Micro-Detail (The Greebles):
   Scale Indicators: Embed tiny technical details to sell the scale.
       Vents: Cooling fans or intake grilles.
       Text: Tiny white serial numbers and warning labels (e.g., "CAUTION: HOT", "NO STEP") printed on the casing.
       The "City" (Optional): If the object is large enough, tiny architectural elements (antennas, platforms) can grow out of the mechanical base.

4. Visual Syntax & Composition:
   Background: Clean Studio Grey (Infinite Curve). The focus is entirely on the object's silhouette.
   Lighting:
       Key Light: Soft white studio light to highlight the texture of the carbon fiber weave.
       Rim Light: A sharp backlight to define the edge of the object against the grey background.
       Bloom: The internal colored LEDs must have a soft "Octane Bloom" effect.

5. Render Style:
   Aesthetic: Hard Surface Modeling, "Tech-Wear" Fashion, High-End Automotive Design.
   Camera: Isometric or 3/4 Product Shot angle.

Output: Photorealistic 3D Render, 8k, Highly Detailed Textures (Carbon Fiber, Brushed Metal, Rubber).
</instructions>
```

### No. 114: Game Asset - Precure Transformation Design System Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed system prompt for Nano Banana Pro that acts as a 'Chief Designer' for a magical girl anime, taking an input character image and generating a 'Precure' transformation design. The prompt dictates every step of the design process, including motif selection, direction, color, naming conventions, hair, costume, eyes, accessories, posing, and the final catchphrase, ensuring the result fits the established Precure aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
# Your Role
You are the chief designer for a girls' anime.
Your mission is to design a character suitable for a girls' anime according to my requests.

# Your Request
Please design the transformed appearance of the character I present as a Precure.
**The design must look natural if it appeared in the Precure series.**

# Design Procedure
Please proceed with the design according to the following flow:

## Motif Determination
Devise a motif that matches the image of the character I presented.
**Capture the character's characteristics and select an appropriate motif.**
**Do not consider elements such as the background of the input image; focus only on the character's characteristics.**
Select the motif from a variety of candidates. For example:
- Nature (sky, earth, sea, etc.)
- Animals (dogs, cats, rabbits, etc.)
- Plants (various flowers, etc.)
- Food (fruits, etc.)
- Emotions (love, joy, etc.)
- Conceptual things (peace, nobility, etc.)

## Direction Determination
Determine the design direction for the character.
**Capture the character's characteristics and find a direction that suits the character.**
For example:
- Cute
- Beautiful
- Brave
- Comical

## Image Color Determination
Determine the character's image color.
**Select a color appropriate for the character's image and the determined motif.**
Colors should be bright and vivid, such as red, blue, yellow, green, purple, and avoid dark colors like brown or gray.
However, black and white can be used if they suit the character's image.

## Name Determination
Determine the character's Precure name.
The name must be Cure â—‹â—‹ (preferably 3 to 6 characters excluding "Cure").
The â—‹â—‹ part should be a name that evokes the character's motif.
(For example, if the motif is a star, use Star, Ã‰toile, Stella, etc.)
Basically, use foreign language words.
Soft-sounding English, French, or Italian words are desirable, and caution is needed when using strong-sounding German or Russian words.
**The name must not overlap with existing Precure names.**

## Character Design Determination
**The design must be suitable as a Precure.**

### Hair
The hair color should be bright and vivid, in the same color family as the original character's hair color.
For example, changes like:
- Red â†’ Pink
- Black â†’ Blue or Green
- Brown â†’ Blonde
The hairstyle is generally an exaggerated, voluminous version of the original character's hairstyle.
However, it is also possible to add elements that the original character does not have (e.g., large twin tails for a short-haired character).

### Outfit
The design is based on the image of the motif. However, avoid designs that are exactly the motif; the design should only suggest the motif.
The color is based on the character's image color.
The character's direction should also be reflected.
For example:
- For a cute direction, use cute designs adorned with frills, etc.
- For a beautiful direction, use streamlined and elegant designs.
- For a brave direction, use sharp and active designs.
- For a comical direction, use pop and cheerful designs.

### Eyes
The eyes should be designed as in the following examples:
- Make the color brighter and more vivid than the original character's.
- Add stars or hearts inside the eyes.

### Accessories
Add accessories such as earrings and tiaras.

### Items
**Since Precure fundamentally fights unarmed, handheld weapons are strictly prohibited.**
They should generally not be holding anything.

## Final Pose
**The pose must be a visually striking pose suitable for a transforming heroine's finishing pose.**
Consider the character's direction (cute, brave, etc.) for the pose design and facial expression during the pose.

## Catchphrase
Devise the character's catchphrase.
The catchphrase should be related to the motif.
Examples:
- Motif is Flower: "A single flower blooming on the earth"
- Motif is Star: "A sparkling star shining in the universe"
- Motif is Sky: "The infinitely spreading blue sky"
**Do not use the examples as is.**

# Final Output
Finish the design determined so far into a single illustration.
The following elements are mandatory:
- The composition should show the designed Precure in their finishing pose.
- The background should be a sparkling space based on the image color, and motifs may be incorporated.
- Write the catchphrase and name at the bottom of the illustration.
  - Divide into 2 lines: 1st line is the catchphrase + "!", 2nd line is the name + "!!".
  - The font should reflect the character's direction. For a cute direction, use cute rounded letters; for a brave direction, use strong letters, etc.
```

</div>

### No. 116: Game Asset - 3D Cinematic Character Render with Adaptive Magic Aura

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A master prompt template for generating a full-body 3D cinematic render of an existing character. It strictly mandates preserving the original identity, design, and color palette from a reference image, while adding subtle, adaptive magical power effects as accents.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Create a full-body 3D cinematic render of the attached reference character, strictly preserving the original identity, design language, and color palette of the uploaded image, while adding subtle magical power effects as accent details only.
Color Direction (CRITICAL â€” FOLLOW REFERENCE EXACTLY)

Maintain the same:
primary colors
contrast levels
saturation balance
material finishes
DO NOT introduce new dominant colors
DO NOT globally darken or color-grade the character
```

### No. 117: Game Asset - Action Figure Transformation Prompt for Nano Banana Pro

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A comprehensive, multi-part prompt designed specifically for Nano Banana Pro to transform a reference character illustration into a highly detailed, photorealistic PVC action figure, displayed in multiple dynamic poses within a catalog-style layout.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
subject:
  The original character from the single reference illustration,
  represented as a highly detailed collectible PVC action figure.
  The characterâ€™s design, proportions, facial features, hairstyle, outfit, and colors are preserved exactly.

composition:
  A single 3:4 frame divided into multiple clearly defined rectangular panels.
  Each panel presents the same action figure posed differently.
  Panels are separated by thin, clean borders in a neutral tone.
  Each figure is centered within its own panel.

action:
  Dynamic action poses made possible by articulated action-figure construction.
  Poses emphasize balance, tension, and expressive movement,
  clearly reading as intentionally posed action figures rather than static statues.

location:
  Neutral studio background with a seamless white to light gray gradient.
  Each panel maintains consistent studio conditions.

style:
  Photorealistic collectible PVC action figure.
  Realistic articulation-friendly sculpting suitable for dynamic posing.

camera_lighting:
  Professional studio lighting consistent across all panels.
  Controlled highlights, sharp focus, shallow depth of field.
  Soft shadows beneath each figure within its panel.

colors:
  Exact color reproduction from the original illustration, unchanged.

edit_instructions:
  Transform this illustration into a photorealistic PVC anime figure.
  Keep the original characterâ€™s design, action pose, and colors exactly the same.
  Render it as a collectible figurine made of PVC plastic, with realistic painted surface and detailed shading.
  Apply glossy highlights on areas such as the hair and clothing.
  Use a matte finish on the skin.
  Add subtle seam lines as seen in real manufactured figures.
  Include transparent plastic figure stands supporting dynamic action poses.
  Do not include opaque bases or decorative display platforms.

extras:
  High-resolution, catalog-quality product image.
```

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
